# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

Converts v0alpha1 dashboards to v1beta1\\n- `v1beta1_to_v2alpha1.go` - Converts v1beta1 dashboards to v2alpha1\\n- `v2alpha1_to_v1beta1.go` - Reverse conversion from v2alpha1 to v1beta1\\n- `v2alpha1_to_v2beta1.go` - Converts v2alpha1 to v2beta1\\n- `v2beta1_to_v2alpha1.go` - Reverse conversion from v2beta1 to v2alpha1\\n- `conversion_data_loss_detection.go` - Detects and tracks data loss during conversions\\n- `errors.go` and `metrics.go` - Supporting infrastructure for legacy storage access\\n\\n### Migration Coordination\\n\\n- `pkg/registry/apis/dashboard/migrator/migrator.go` - Implements `FoldersDashboardsMigrator` interface via `foldersDashboardsMigrator` struct and `ProvideFoldersDashboardsMigrator()` function\\n- `pkg/registry/apis/dashboard/migration_registrar.go` - Schema validation using `ValidateDashboardSpec()`\\n- `apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/v0alpha1/conversion.go`, `v1beta1/conversion.go`, `v2alpha1/conversion.go`, `v2beta1/conversion.go` - Generated and manual conversion implementations\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Dual-Path Migration**: Dashboards can be migrated either on the frontend (older versions) or backend (newer versions), with careful coordination to avoid double migration.\\n\\n2. **Field-Level Migrations**: Individual migration functions handle specific schema version changes, from simple property moves (v2) to complex datasource reference transformations (v33) to field configuration updates (v42).\\n\\n3. **Frontend Defaults Application**: The backend explicitly applies frontend DashboardModel and PanelModel constructor defaults to ensure consistency between frontend and backend processing.\\n\\n4. **Datasource Index Caching**: Migrations that reference datasources use a cached indexing system for efficient O(1) lookups.\\n\\n5. **Conversion Status Tracking**: The conversion layer tracks conversion metadata including source/target versions and any errors that occurred.\\n\\n6. **Version Pinning**: Schema version 42 is explicitly marked as final, with future panel-specific migrations to be implemented in individual panel plugin migration handlers rather than as new dashboard schema versions.\\n\"\n}\n",

Defines `SchemaVersionMigrationFunc` type and constants `LATEST_VERSION = 42` and `MIN_VERSION = 0`.\\n- `schemaversion/errors.go` - Error types including `MigrationError` and `MinimumVersionError`\\n- `schemaversion/v2.go` through `schemaversion/v42.go` - Individual migration functions (V2-V42) for each schema version. TTL-based caching mechanism with `cachedProvider` type for indexing datasources and library elements\\n- `schemaversion/datasource_utils.go` - `DatasourceIndex` for O(1) datasource lookups, `WrapIndexProviderWithCache()` for caching provider results\\n\\n### Conversion Layer\\n\\nThe conversion layer in `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/conversion/` handles transformations between different API versions:\\n\\n- `conversion.go` -
